<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пекарня.html>пека́рня</a> (20665)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пекарь.html>пе́карь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pékarʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">пькъло</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pĭkŭlo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>scorching heat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пекло.html>пе́кло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лице</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nu i <b>péklo</b> na úlice!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What a scorcher outside!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> heat (the height or stress of an action or condition)

<li>hell

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:печься.html>пеку́щийся</a> (19330)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пелена.html>пелена́</a> (8861)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pelena</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пелена.html>пелена́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pelená</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пелена.html>пелены́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пелена.html>пелены́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пелена.html>пелён</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shroud
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снежный.html>сне́жная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пелена.html>пелена́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">snéžnaja <b>pelená</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">mantle of snow</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пелена.html>пелена́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаз</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:упасть.html>упа́ла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó slóvno <b>pelená</b> s glaz upála</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the scales fell from his eyes</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пенал.html>пена́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">penál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пенал.html>пена́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пенал.html>пена́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пенал.html>пена́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pencil case, pencil box <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">object purposed to contain stationery</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пенальти.html>пена́льти</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">penálʹti</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
